(function() {
  function getCookie(name) {
    if (name) {
      var cookieRegex = new RegExp(name + "=([^\\s;]*)");
      var sMatch = document.cookie.match(cookieRegex);
      if (sMatch && sMatch[1]) {
        return decodeURIComponent(sMatch[1]);
      }
    }
    return "";
  }

  function get(path, obj) {
    try {
      var val;
      var paths = typeof path === "string" ? path.split(".") : path;
      if (obj && typeof obj === "object") {
        paths.forEach(function(k, i) {
          if (i === 0) {
            val = obj[k];
          } else if (val) {
            val = val[k];
          }
        });
      }
      return val;
    } catch (e) {
      // In case of an error, prevents side effects on page level
      return;
    }
  }

  function getAppName() {
    return get("_wml.config.ui.applicationName", window);
  }

  function getMidasConfig() {
    return get("_wml.config.ccm.midasConfig", window) || {};
  }
  function getMidasUiConfig() {
    return get("_wml.config.ui.midasConfig", window) || {};
  }

  function getMidasCfgVal(cfgName) {
    var cfg = getMidasConfig();
    var appName = getAppName();
    var pageCfgKey = appName + "-" + cfgName;
    return cfg[pageCfgKey] || cfg[cfgName];
  }

  function loadScript(scriptUrl) {
    var script = document.createElement("script");
    script.async = true;
    script.src = scriptUrl;
    document.head.appendChild(script);
  }

  function loadAds() {
    if (!loadAds.loaded) {
      addPerfMark("load-midas-display");
      loadAds.loaded = true;
      var displayAds = getMidasCfgVal("displayAds") !== "false";
      if (displayAds) {
        var MDABT = getCookie("MDABT");
        var midasDisplayScript =
          getMidasCfgVal("test-" + MDABT) ||
          getMidasCfgVal("midasDisplayScript");
        var gptUrl = "//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js";
        if (getMidasCfgVal("loadDisplayScript") !== "false") {
          loadScript(midasDisplayScript);
        }
        loadScript(gptUrl);
      }
    }
  }

  function loadS2SScripts() {
    if (!loadS2SScripts.loaded) {
      addPerfMark("load-s2s-midas-scripts");
      loadS2SScripts.loaded = true;
      var MDABTS2S = getCookie("MDABTS2S");
      var midasS2SScript =
        getMidasCfgVal("test-" + MDABTS2S) || getMidasCfgVal("midasS2SScript");
      loadScript(midasS2SScript);
    }
  }

  function addPerfMark(markName){
    var hasPerfMark = !!get("performance.mark", window);
    if (hasPerfMark) {
      // For some reason it causes an error when you store the reference of the mark fn.
      window.performance.mark(markName);
    }
  }
  var loadS2SEvent =
    getCookie("loadS2SEvent") ||
    getMidasUiConfig()["loadS2SEvent"] ||
    getMidasCfgVal("loadS2SEvent") ||
    "hasS2SPayload";

  var loadEvent =
    getCookie("loadEvent") ||
    getMidasUiConfig()["loadEvent"] ||
    getMidasCfgVal("loadEvent") ||
    "instant";
  window._wml.adLoader = (function() {
    var eventListeners = {};
    return {
      fireEvent: function fireEvent(eventName) {
        addPerfMark('fire-event-' + eventName);
        var listeners = eventListeners[eventName];

        if (listeners) {
          listeners.forEach(function(listener) {
            listener();
          });
        }
      },
      subscribe: function subscribe(eventName, listener) {
        if (!eventListeners[eventName]) {
          eventListeners[eventName] = [];
        }

        eventListeners[eventName].push(listener);
      },
    };
  })();

  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadEvent, loadAds);
  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadS2SEvent, loadS2SScripts);
  _wml.adLoader.fireEvent("instant"); // Default load ads immediately
})();

var applicationName = _wml.config.ui.applicationName || "default";

Plays all size records. I use mine for portable bedroom use. I play older 50s 60s 70s 80s records on it. Mostly albums. And im happy with the results. Keep in mind, this player is for fun daily use. I use it almost daily to listen to one of my vinyl records. The turntable was so easy to use that I didn&#39;t even need to read the instructions, I was using it as soon as I unpacked it and plugged it in. </p><p>You are able to play 33, 45, and 78 RPM records with the speed switch. Not only does this turntable play you vinyl records you can connect any bluetooth device and enjoy your music through the unit. It also has an auxiliary jack but I have yet to have a need for it.</p><p>There is also a headphone jack should you not want to share your music or bother anyone. With this turntable, you also have a pitch control and auto-stop which are nice added features. </p><p>The case which contains the turntable is well made, stylish and you can close it when you are listening with your bluetooth device without any sound interruption. If you were carrying your turntable with you the case reminds me of a briefcase, so no one would ever guess you had tunes with you!</p></div></div><div itemprop="name" class="review-title font-bold">Great record player for the price</h3></div><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/Rating"><meta itemprop="worstRating" content="1"/><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></div><div class="review-date"><span itemprop="datePublished" content="May 18, 2020" is a great little record player to have. It&#39;s not high end, or fancy, but it gets the job done. Some people might say that if you want better sound quality, that you need to buy a really expensive record playing. I say if you want good quality, just listen to an mp3. </p><p>What I like about playing records is the ritual. This record player has great aesthetics with the red interior. It looks great, and it sounds great. It&#39;s easy to use, I have nothing bad to say about it. </p><p>I like how it has a lot of optional inputs. The AUX is cool, and convenient. You can also use it as a Bluetooth speaker which is pretty cool. </p><p>My favorite thing about it is the pitch knob. My old record player&#39;s belt stretched, and it wasn&#39;t adjustable. Those belts are a real pain to change too. The fact that I can adjust it with a knob is great.</p><p>I turned it up, and it sounds good at any volume.</p></div></div><div </span><span class="visuallyhidden seo-best-rating">5</span><span class="visuallyhidden"> stars</span></div></div><h3 itemprop="name" class="review-title font-bold">Bummer</h3></div><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/Rating"><meta itemprop="worstRating" content="1"/><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></div><div class="review-date"><span itemprop="datePublished" content="May 13, 2020" class="review-date-submissionTime">May 13, 2020</span></div><div class="review-body"><div itemprop="reviewBody" class="review-description"><div><div class="collapsable content-fadeout review-body-text has-toggle" style="min-height:125px" id="Collapsable-1628895598540"><div class="collapsable-content-container"><div><div class="review-text"><p>I had high expectations for this, it&#39;s been so long since I&#39;ve been able to listen to my records (plus this has Bluetooth capabilities!) but sadly I was let down. On first glance I can tell these are just mass produced junk by the crooked handle (see pic) and the way the cover was already worn and not stretched properly on the open edges. Unfortunately I was only able to attach 2 pictures so I couldn&#39;t fully showcase the flaws. The player is lightweight, which is a plus if you plan on moving it around often (hence the handle and suitcase style??) but to me that just means it&#39;s basic. I first used it as a Bluetooth speaker and played songs from my phone, the speakers are okay but I noticed they sounded better with the case closed (which you can&#39;t do with a bigger record btw). I would compare it to one of the shower speakers you can buy. Then I tried one of my older hair metal records and heard no change in the sound, clear but dull and flat. I think the needle is very flimsy and will probably need replaced quickly and often but at least mine came intact unlike other reviewers. Overall the look is cool, I dig the red on black, and it works but if you want the real experience I&#39;d keep looking.</p></div></div><div
